  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Expense Management Status Report;
    OnInitReport=VAR
                   EMSetup@1000 : Record 6086300;
                   Language@1001 : Record 8;
                 BEGIN
                   DateFilter := STRSUBSTNO('..%1',CALCDATE('<CM-1M+1D>',WORKDATE));
                   IncludeNotPosted := TRUE;
                   IncludePosted := TRUE;

                   EMSetup.GET;
                   CurrReport.LANGUAGE := Language.GetLanguageID(EMSetup."Default Web/App Language");
                 END;

    OnPreReport=VAR
                  EMSetup@1000 : Record 6086300;
                  GLSetup@1001 : Record 98;
                BEGIN
                  EMSetup.GET;
                  GLSetup.GET;
                  DistanceUnit := FORMAT(EMSetup."Distance Unit");
                  LCYCode := GLSetup."LCY Code";
                END;

    PreviewMode=PrintLayout;
  }

    { 39  ;0   ;DataItem;                    ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086001;
               PrintOnlyIfDetail=Yes;
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               UserResp@1000 : Record 6086379;
                             BEGIN
                               IF UserResp.GetResponsibilityFilter <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                 "Continia User".FILTERGROUP(2);
                                 "Continia User".SETFILTER("User ID",UserResp.GetResponsibilityFilter);
                                 "Continia User".FILTERGROUP(0);
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF NOT ContiniaUserSetup.GET("Continia User"."User ID") THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;
                                  ContiniaUserSetup.CALCFIELDS("Vendor Balance (LCY)");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 8   ;1   ;DataItem;Expenses            ;
               DataItemTable=Table6086320;
               DataItemTableView=;
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF SettlementNo <> '' THEN
                                 Expenses.SETFILTER("Settlement No.",SettlementNo);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  ExpenseTmp@1000 : Record 6086320;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (NOT IncludePosted) AND Expenses.Posted THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF (NOT IncludeNotPosted) AND (NOT Expenses.Posted) THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF DateFilter <> '' THEN
                                    IF Expenses.Posted THEN BEGIN
                                      ExpenseTmp.RESET;
                                      ExpenseTmp.SETRANGE("Entry No.",Expenses."Entry No.");
                                      ExpenseTmp.SETFILTER("Document Date",DateFilter);
                                      IF ExpenseTmp.ISEMPTY THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP;
                                    END;

                                  IF Expenses."No Refund" THEN BEGIN
                                    Expenses.Amount := -Expenses.Amount;
                                    Expenses."Amount (LCY)" := -Expenses."Amount (LCY)";
                                  END;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Continia User ID,Document Date;
               DataItemLink=Continia User ID=FIELD(User ID) }

    LOCAL PROCEDURE MakePeriodFilter@1160040002(VAR Period@1160040000 : Text[30]);
    VAR
      DateRec@1160040002 : Record 2000000007;
      AppMgt@1160040001 : Codeunit 1;
    BEGIN
      AppMgt.MakeDateFilter(Period);
      DateRec.SETRANGE("Period Type",DateRec."Period Type"::Date);
      DateRec.SETFILTER("Period Start",Period);
      Period := DateRec.GETFILTER("Period Start");
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetGlobalVars@2(InclPosted@1000 : Boolean;InclNotPosted@1001 : Boolean;DateFlt@1002 : Text[30]);
    BEGIN
      IncludePosted := InclPosted;
      IncludeNotPosted := InclNotPosted;
      DateFilter := DateFlt;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
